article</a>.</p><h3 class="wt-text-caption-title wt-mb-xs-2 wt-mt-xs-2">Listing videos</h3><ul class="wt-list wt-text-caption"><li>Most file types are accepted.</li><li>Max file size is id="popover-content-a3d4eada-ef07-47b6-8849-d2e8d11fd6b6"><h3 class="wt-text-caption-title wt-mb-xs-1">Tips for a great title:</h3><ul class="wt-mb-xs-2"><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Clearly state the item for sale, like "mug" or "dress"</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Include the most important traits upfront, like your item's color, material, and size</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Streamline for clarity and scannability. Consider using less than 15 words when including the traits that make your item special.</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Only include holidays, special occasions, or recipient types if they're essential to what the item is, like "birthday candle" or "Halloween costume"</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Move subjective words, like "perfect" or "beautiful," to the description</li><li class="wt-text-caption wt-mb-xs-1">Try not to repeat words</li><li class="wt-text-caption">Don't worry about adding info about price, shipping, or sales. Etsy helps take care of this by badging your items in Search.</li></ul><p class="wt-mb-xs-2 wt-mt-xs-2 wt-text-caption">Note that the first title you publish will be used in the listing URL, even if Selling items you designed, made, or modified? You’re probably the manufacturer.</p><p class="wt-mt-xs-2 wt-text-caption"> Selling second-hand items in their original condition?
